Periodic requalification studies may be performed based on risk assessments, site validation procedures, or changes in the ongoing trend data or as required by local regulations (e.g., current version of Annex 1 recommends requalification of Grade A & B every 6 months and Grade C & D every 12 months.)

        

The change control for the affected rooms should assess cumulative changes in the rooms that may warrant requalification. An EMPQ study protocol should include the scope and requirements of the requalification, sampling plan, and acceptance criteria.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Requalification (再確效)：**不是「重做一次 EMPQ」，而是針對特定變更所做的確認性研究。觸發條件包括：

            

                
- 結構性變更（牆壁、天花板、地板更換）

                
- 製程流程改變

                
- 建材變更 (materials of construction)

                
- 區域用途改變（如從 Grade C 包裝區改為 Grade B 配液區）

                
- CCS 程序變更（消毒計畫、著裝程序等）

                
- 趨勢數據出現變化

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**EU GMP Annex 1 的週期性再確效要求：**

            
                
| 潔淨等級 | 再確效週期 |
| --- | --- |
                
| Grade A & B | 每 6 個月 |
                
| Grade C & D | 每 12 個月 |
            

            

這是 Annex 1 的明確建議。值得注意的是，Change Control 程序需要評估「累積性變更」——也就是說，單獨看每一個小變更可能不需要再確效，但多個小變更累積起來的效應可能需要。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

再確效就像汽車的定期保養檢測。即使你的車開起來好好的，每半年或一萬公里還是要回廠檢查。如果你換了引擎零件（重大變更），就要立刻回廠驗車；如果只是換了雨刷（小變更），可能不用，但如果你同時換了雨刷、胎壓感測器、又調了方向盤角度，這些累積起來就該整體檢查一次了。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果一個 Grade B 區域在過去6個月內進行了三次小型維修（更換一塊天花板板材、調整回風口位置、更換一盞 UV 燈），是否需要再確效？你會如何評估？

                
2. 為什麼 Annex 1 對 Grade A/B 的再確效週期（6個月）比 Grade C/D（12個月）更頻繁？風險的差異在哪裡？

            

        

    

## 7.1.2 Environmental Monitoring Critical Parameters

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

The HVAC system and associated air handling units control the cleanliness of the air and provide an environment that is suitable for operators to work safely and comfortably. Procedures should be in place to monitor and trend critical parameters to assess whether the cleanroom is performing as intended. The procedures should also include instructions on how to handle excursions and alarms. Critical parameters are outlined in Sections 7.1.2.1–7.1.2.3.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**HVAC System (暖通空調系統)：**潔淨室的「生命維持系統」。它不只控制空氣清潔度，還要同時為操作人員提供安全、舒適的工作環境。三大關鍵參數（即後續小節說明的氣流模式、壓差、溫濕度）都由 HVAC 系統管控。

            

**Excursions (偏移)：**當關鍵參數超出設定限度時的事件。程序中必須包含偏移處理與警報應對的明確指引。

        

    

## 7.1.2.1 Air Patterns, Air Movement, and Air Changes

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

Airflow patterns in critical zones and the background environment need to be studied during qualification to show that air turbulence does not interfere with aseptic processes during static or dynamic conditions. There are two types of air flow patterns: turbulent flow and unidirectional flow.

        

Turbulent airflow is used in most classified areas other than Grade A environments; it is designed to dilute particles and microorganisms in cleanrooms and keep them suspended in the air until they are removed with new "clean" air. The number of air changes per hour of a cleanroom is related to the extent to which potential contaminants can be removed from the room. Each grade of cleanroom should meet a preset number of air changes per hour based on a risk assessment performed as part of the EMPQ. Airflow visualization studies may be conducted in areas of turbulent airflow such as cleanrooms to optimize the layout, use and monitoring locations.

        

Unidirectional airflow is applied in higher classified areas (i.e., Grade A) and is designed to sweep particles and microorganisms away from critical operations, ensuring that the "first air" is never contaminated before it comes in contact with the product (the critical zone). Airflow visualization studies are designed to demonstrate that unidirectional airflow is delivered to the working position by the BSC or barrier system, and that the product is only exposed to "first air" during operations. Airflow visualization studies are also performed in areas that adjacent to the critical zone to ensure air is not moving into the aseptic area, e.g., air entering through the mouseholes or depyrogenation tunnel into a barrier system, or air passing through the air curtain of a BSC. PDA Technical Report No. 62: *Recommended Practices for Manual Aseptic Processes* and EU GMP Annex 1: *Manufacture of Sterile Medicinal Products* also discuss airflow in aseptic manufacturing areas.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Turbulent Airflow (亂流氣流)：**用於 Grade B/C/D 等大部分潔淨區域。原理是透過大量換氣「稀釋」空氣中的微粒和微生物，使其懸浮後隨新鮮空氣排出。每小時換氣次數 (ACH, Air Changes per Hour) 越高，稀釋能力越強。

            

**Unidirectional Airflow (單向氣流)：**用於 Grade A 關鍵區域。原理完全不同——不是稀釋，而是「掃除」。空氣以均勻、平行的方式流動，將微粒和微生物從關鍵操作區域「吹走」，確保產品只接觸到「第一氣流」(First Air)。

            

**First Air (第一氣流)：**指從 HEPA 過濾器出來後、尚未接觸任何物體或人員的潔淨空氣。產品在關鍵操作期間只能暴露於 first air，這是無菌保證的核心原則之一。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像兩種清潔地板的方式：

            

                
- **亂流 = 用水沖洗浴室：**大量的水沖進去，髒東西被水流帶動、稀釋，最後從排水孔流走。水量越大，沖得越乾淨。

                
- **單向流 = 用掃把從一端掃到另一端：**所有灰塵都被有方向性地推到一邊去，不會來回擾動。你站在掃把前方（first air 的位置），永遠不會碰到灰塵。

            

            

Mouseholes（傳送窗口）就像門縫——如果沒有正確的氣流方向，外面走廊的灰塵就會從門縫鑽進手術室。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**氣流可視化 (Smoke Study) 的關鍵檢查點：**

            

                
- Grade A 區域：確認單向氣流確實送達工作位置，產品只暴露於 first air

                
- Grade A 鄰接區域：確認無外部空氣侵入（如 mouseholes、去熱原隧道、BSC 的氣簾）

                
- 亂流區域：優化佈局與監測點位置

                
- 必須在靜態與動態兩種條件下執行

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼 Grade A 使用單向流而不是大幅增加亂流的換氣次數？兩者在「保護產品」的原理上有何本質差異？

                
2. 如果 smoke study 顯示充填區有一個小區域存在渦流 (vortex)，這代表什麼風險？應如何處理？

            

        

    

## 7.1.2.2 Differential Air Pressure

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

Air pressurization will ensure airflow from a higher to a lower cleanliness level by maintaining positive pressure in the areas of higher classification. Air visualization performed in both static and dynamic conditions will demonstrate appropriate pressure differential. In viral-vector manufacturing, guidance on differential pressure between rooms of different classification can be found in U.S. FDA Guidance for Industry: *Sterile Drug Products Produced by Aseptic Processing — Current Good Manufacturing Practice*, EU GMP Annex 1 *Manufacture of Sterile Medicinal Products*, and PDA Technical Report No. 13 (Revised 2021): *Fundamentals of an Environmental Monitoring Program*.

        

In the case of high-potency products, both active egress from the area and contamination of the product should be prevented. This can be achieved by applying air locks with different pressures between areas of different classification. Pressure differentials should be monitored with an alarm mechanism for minimum and maximum pressure limits.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Pressure Differential (壓差)：**透過維持較高等級區域的正壓，確保空氣永遠從較潔淨的區域流向較不潔淨的區域。這是防止外部污染物侵入的物理屏障。

            

**High-Potency Products (高效能/高活性產品)：**面臨雙重挑戰——既要防止外部污染進入產品（正壓保護），又要防止高效能物質擴散到外部環境（負壓圍堵）。解決方案是使用具有不同壓力的 Air Locks (氣閘) 在不同分類區域之間建立壓力梯度。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

壓差就像「風向」的人為控制。想像一棟大樓的每一層都有不同氣壓：頂樓氣壓最高，每往下一層就低一點。這樣空氣永遠是從上往下流，灰塵不可能逆流上去。潔淨室的壓差原理完全一樣——最乾淨的房間壓力最高，「空氣門」永遠朝外推。

            

高效能產品的情況更像生物安全實驗室 (BSL)：你既不想讓外面的細菌進來污染你的實驗，也不想讓裡面的危險病原跑出去。這時就需要「三明治」結構的氣閘——中間是緩衝區，分別用不同壓力來控制兩個方向的氣流。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**壓差監測必須配備警報機制：**需設定最低和最高壓力限值，當壓差偏離時立即觸發警報。這不是建議，而是基本要求。壓差的喪失意味著污染屏障的瓦解，可能導致整批產品報廢。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果你負責設計一個同時生產高效能抗癌藥物的無菌充填區，壓差策略應該如何規劃？畫出各區域的壓力梯度圖。

                
2. 為什麼壓差監測需要同時設定「最低」和「最高」限值？過高的壓差會造成什麼問題？

            

        

    

## 7.1.2.3 Temperature and Relative Humidity

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

Products may be affected by temperature and humidity, and these parameters are important for operator comfort as well. Shivering or excess perspiration on the part of an operator may result in the release of a higher number of particles into the cleanroom than an operator's garments can retain, which may contaminate the environment. Temperature and humidity levels also have an impact on microbial proliferation. Both parameters should be monitored against their set limits.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**溫濕度的雙重角色：**溫度和相對濕度影響兩個面向：

            

                
- **產品面：**某些產品（如生物製劑、蛋白質藥物）對溫濕度敏感

                
- **人員面：**操作人員太冷會發抖、太熱會流汗，兩者都會導致釋放更多微粒到潔淨室中，超出無塵衣的攔截能力

                
- **微生物面：**高溫高濕有利於微生物增殖

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

溫濕度控制就像手術室的溫度設定——外科醫生穿著厚重的手術衣和手套，如果室溫太高會大量出汗，手可能打滑；如果太冷會手指僵硬，影響精細操作。無菌操作的道理完全一樣：操作人員的舒適度直接影響他們作為「污染源」的風險等級。一個流汗的操作員產生的微粒量可能是正常狀態的數倍。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

溫濕度往往被視為「次要參數」而被忽略，但本節明確指出它對污染控制有直接影響。特別注意：操作人員著裝後（穿上無塵衣、戴手套、護目鏡），體感溫度會比環境溫度高出許多。因此潔淨室的溫度設定不能只考慮產品需求，還必須考慮穿著完整無塵衣後的人體舒適範圍。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果 Grade B 區域的相對濕度從 45% 上升到 70%，可能帶來哪些污染控制風險？

                
2. 在撰寫 CCS 文件時，溫濕度監測應歸類在哪個控制要素下？應如何設定行動限值 (action limits)？

            

        

    

## 7.2 Environment and Utility Disruption and Recovery Plan

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

When a disruption occurs in a controlled, classified environment or to a critical utility, the risk of contamination is inherently higher than during daily operations. For this reason, a containment strategy for disruptions and a recovery plan should be established with the aim of reducing the contamination risk.

        

A disruption to the controlled, classified environment or critical utility may be planned or unplanned:

        

            
- **Planned disruptions** are deliberate, scheduled events, for example, construction projects, annual shutdown, preventive maintenance, equipment installation

            
- **Unplanned disruptions** are unexpected events, such as leaks in critical utilities, loss of power, or equipment repair, and should be addressed immediately

        

        

The level of containment and recovery should be commensurate with the risk. It is useful to define tiers of risk and outline the appropriate containment strategy and response plan for each tier. An example is presented in Section 17.0–Appendix III.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Disruption (中斷事件)：**指潔淨環境或關鍵公用設施（如注射用水系統 WFI、純蒸汽、壓縮空氣、HVAC）發生的任何干擾，可分為：

            

                
- **Planned (計畫性)：**建築工程、年度停機保養、預防性維護、設備安裝等已排程的事件

                
- **Unplanned (非計畫性)：**公用設施洩漏、斷電、緊急設備維修等突發事件，必須立即處理

            

            

**Recovery Plan (復原計畫)：**定義從中斷到恢復「受控狀態」所需的步驟。圍堵 (Containment) 與復原的力度應與風險相稱 (commensurate with risk)。

            

**Tiers of Risk (風險分級)：**將不同類型和嚴重程度的中斷事件分級，每一級對應不同的圍堵策略與應變計畫。詳見 Section 17.0 Appendix III 的範例。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

中斷與復原計畫就像醫院的緊急應變分級制度：

            

                
- **計畫性中斷 = 排程手術：**提前準備好所有資源、排好時程、通知所有相關人員，事後有計畫地清潔和復原。

                
- **非計畫性中斷 = 緊急送醫：**沒有預警，必須立即啟動應急程序，邊處理邊評估風險。

            

            

風險分級就像醫院的「檢傷分類」(triage)——不是每個中斷事件都需要全面重新確效，輕微的可能只需加強監測，嚴重的可能需要停線、清潔、再確效後才能復產。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**「與風險相稱」(Commensurate with Risk) 是關鍵原則：**

            

                
- 過度反應（每次小中斷都全面停線重新確效）= 浪費資源、降低產能

                
- 反應不足（嚴重中斷只做最低限度處理）= 污染風險，可能導致產品召回

                
- 正確做法是預先建立風險分級表 (risk tier matrix)，讓所有人員在事件發生時能快速、一致地做出判斷

            

            

Annex 1 特別強調，計畫性中斷也必須有正式的控制程序——不能因為「是排程好的」就放鬆管控。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

作為 CDMO，你的設施可能同時服務多個客戶。當發生 HVAC 異常（如 AHU 故障導致 Grade B 區域壓差喪失 30 分鐘）時，你需要：

            

                
1. 依據預定的風險分級表判斷此事件屬於哪一級

                
2. 啟動對應級別的圍堵策略（如隔離受影響區域、暫停操作）

                
3. 執行復原程序（如額外清潔消毒、加強 EM 取樣）

                
4. 評估對所有在製批次的影響，並通知各客戶

                
5. 完成偏差調查、記錄根因並更新 CAPA

            

            

沒有預建風險分級表的工廠，每次都會陷入「臨時判斷」的混亂，不同班次的處理方式可能完全不一致。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 請為一個無菌充填工廠設計三級風險分級表（低/中/高），列出每一級的典型事件、圍堵策略和復原要求。

                
2. 計畫性中斷（如年度停機保養）和非計畫性中斷（如突然斷電），在 CCS 文件中應分別如何記載？復原要求有何不同？

                
3. 如果 WFI 系統在充填作業期間發生溫度偏移（降到 70°C 以下），這屬於什麼等級的中斷？應採取哪些立即行動？

            

        

    

    

### 本節重點回顧 Section Summary

    

        
- **環境控制是 CCS 的基礎：**環境污染物（季節性黴菌、產孢菌、人員皮膚菌）可透過空氣和表面傳播，直接挑戰設施清潔、設備滅菌和無菌操作控制

        
- **EM 是「測量」而非「控制」：**環境監測計畫提供環境品質的離散快照，用於量測控制措施績效並預警失控，但絕不能用良好的 EM 趨勢來辯護降低控制標準

        
- **EMPQ 是 EM 的基石：**在新建或重大變更後的潔淨區域執行 EMPQ，其結果直接決定日常 EM 計畫的取樣策略和監測點位

        
- **再確效有明確觸發條件：**結構/製程/建材變更、用途變更、CCS 程序變更、趨勢變化，以及 Annex 1 要求的週期性再確效（A/B 級每6個月、C/D 級每12個月）

        
- **三大 HVAC 關鍵參數：**氣流模式（亂流稀釋 vs. 單向流掃除）、壓差（正壓防護+高效能產品的雙向控制）、溫濕度（產品穩定性+操作人員舒適度+微生物增殖）

        
- **中斷與復原必須預先規劃：**區分計畫性與非計畫性中斷，建立風險分級表，圍堵與復原力度與風險相稱，避免過度反應或反應不足

## Section 6: Personnel Training 人員訓練 (p26-p30)

# Section 8.0 Personnel Training and Qualification

    

人員訓練與資格確認

    

PDA Technical Report No. 90: Contamination Control Strategy Development in Pharmaceutical Manufacturing | p26 - p30

    

### 本章學習目標

    

        
- 理解人員訓練與資格確認在污染控制策略 (CCS) 中的核心角色與最低要求

        
- 掌握基礎微生物學訓練的必要內容及其對品質文化的影響

        
- 了解更衣資格確認 (Gowning Qualification)、取消資格 (Disqualification) 與重新確認 (Requalification) 的標準流程

        
- 學習潔淨室行為規範的具體要求，包括無菌操作員訓練與無菌觀察員計畫

        
- 認識從「非全面性」到「全面性 (Holistic)」人員管理思維的轉變

    

    

### 本節目錄

    

        8.0 Personnel Training
        8.1 Basic Microbiology
        8.2 Personal Hygiene
        8.3 Gowning
        8.3.1 Gowning Qualification
        8.3.2 Disqualification & Requalification
        8.4 Cleanroom Behavior
        8.4.1 Aseptic Operator Training
        8.4.2 Aseptic Observer Program
    

## 8.0 Personnel Training and Qualification

    

        

## Original Text

        

Before individuals can enter manufacturing areas, they should have received appropriate training in a standard curriculum for manufacturing personnel. The curriculum should be designed to the role the trainee will be expected to perform. Personnel training and qualification programs should include at a minimum an explanation of the underlying principles and rationale for the controls regarding:

        

            
- Basic Microbiology (see Section 8.1)

            
- Personnel, personnel flow, and associated requirements (see Section 5.2; Section 15.0, Table 6)

            
- Material and waste flow (see Section 5.3; Section 15.0, Table 4)

            
- Environmental controls (see Section 7.0)

            
- Cleaning and Disinfection (see Section 5.1.4)

            
- Process design (see Section 4.0)

        

        

A key element of a microbial contamination control strategy is a routinely scheduled, validated cleaning and disinfection process. The microbiology training program should encompass a clear explanation of the difference between cleaning and disinfection in that the former is purposed to remove physical and chemical residues and the latter is purposed to kill microorganisms. The training program should include an overview of the different cleaning and disinfectant agents and why each are used.

        

Basic microbiology, personal hygiene, gowning, and cleanroom behavior are core topics within a robust contamination control training program. Operators performing activities in the aseptic processing areas should have additional aseptic operator training and meet qualification requirements, including reviewing the airflow visualization studies. Table 8.0-1 highlights the mindset shift toward holistic CCS relating to personnel.

        

            
                Table 8.0-1 — Holistic Approach to Personnel Considerations
                
                    
                    
                
| Non-Holistic Approach | Holistic Approach |
| --- | --- |
                
                    
                    
                
| Contamination cannot occur if SOP instructions and batch records are precisely followed by personnel | Contamination can be prevented by understanding and reducing the specific hazards throughout the process, through a combination of strong CCS practices, quality culture, and continuous improvement |
            

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Personnel Training and Qualification (人員訓練與資格確認)：**這是 CCS 中針對「人」這個最大污染源的系統性管控機制。TR90 要求在人員進入製造區域之前，必須完成一套涵蓋微生物學、個人衛生、更衣、潔淨室行為等核心主題的標準課程。

            

**Cleaning vs. Disinfection (清潔 vs. 消毒)：**清潔的目的是去除物理和化學殘留物；消毒的目的是殺死微生物。訓練計畫必須清楚區分這兩個概念，因為許多操作員容易混淆。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像一家醫院的感染管控計畫 -- 在醫護人員進入手術室之前，他們不僅需要知道「怎麼做」(SOP)，更需要理解「為什麼這樣做」。一位只會機械式遵循步驟的護士，在遇到異常狀況時可能不知如何應變；而一位真正理解微生物傳播原理的護士，即使在非標準情境下也能做出正確判斷。這就是 Table 8.0-1 中「非全面性」與「全面性」方法的核心差異。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**思維轉變的關鍵：**傳統觀念認為「只要精確遵循 SOP 和批次記錄，就不會發生污染」。但全面性方法認為，光遵循程序是不夠的 -- 人員必須理解整個製程中的具體危害，並結合 CCS 實務、品質文化和持續改善來預防污染。

            

訓練課程應「依角色設計」(designed to the role)，這意味著不同職位的人員接受不同深度的訓練，而非一體適用。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 環境中，由於客戶產品多樣、製程頻繁轉換，人員訓練的挑戰更大。一個有效的做法是建立「模組化訓練矩陣」：基礎模組 (微生物學、衛生、更衣) 為所有人員必修，而進階模組 (無菌操作、特定製程) 則依角色選配。這樣既確保全面覆蓋，又能靈活適應不同產品線的需求。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼 TR90 強調人員必須理解「原理與理由」而非僅僅遵循 SOP？這對實際污染預防有何影響？

                
2. 在你的工廠中，清潔 (cleaning) 和消毒 (disinfection) 的訓練是否有清楚區分？操作員能否正確解釋兩者的差異？

            

        

    

## 8.1 Basic Microbiology

    

        

## Original Text

        

Microbiology is the science and study of microorganisms. Microorganisms can potentially impact pharmaceutical facilities, manufacturing processes, and finished drug products. An education program of basic microbiology should be integrated into the employee training that explains the various types of microorganisms (minimally, bacteria, yeasts, and molds). This would describe how microorganisms may cause an impact through contamination, including proliferation, and their potential to release toxins (including endotoxins), and why this can impact patient safety based on the types of finished drug products, patient population and the route of drug administration.

        

The program should explain the main sources of microorganisms, including people, utilities (e.g., water, gases), the environment, and raw materials. A comprehensive microbiology training program would also include a description of viruses and prions, their origins, their sources, and how and where they might impact the manufacturing process and finished drug product quality. This should also include any requirements for TSE and BSE statements for all materials that pose a potential risk of contamination from prions.

        

When employees understand the sources and potential consequences of contamination from microorganisms, they are more capable to prevent contaminations and build practices that support a proactive quality culture related to contamination control.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Basic Microbiology (基礎微生物學)：**微生物學訓練的最低要求涵蓋三大類微生物：

            

                
- **Bacteria (細菌)：**最常見的污染源，可快速增殖並釋放內毒素 (endotoxins)

                
- **Yeasts (酵母菌)：**真菌的一種，常見於環境和人體

                
- **Molds (黴菌)：**真菌的另一種，可透過孢子在空氣中傳播

            

            

進階訓練還應涵蓋 Viruses (病毒) 和 Prions (朊病毒)，後者與 TSE (傳染性海綿狀腦病) 和 BSE (牛海綿狀腦病) 相關。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

微生物學訓練就像教駕訓班學員認識各種道路危害 -- 你不能只告訴他們「紅燈停、綠燈行」，你還需要讓他們了解為什麼闖紅燈危險（交通事故的後果）、道路上有哪些潛在危險（行人、腳踏車、施工區），以及在不同情境下如何正確判斷。當操作員真正理解微生物的來源和危害，他們就會從「被動遵守規則」轉變為「主動預防污染」。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**四大微生物來源：**People (人員)、Utilities (公用系統，如水、氣體)、Environment (環境)、Raw Materials (原料)。記住這四個來源是理解整個 CCS 的基礎。

            

**Proactive Quality Culture (主動品質文化)：**TR90 明確指出，當員工理解污染的來源和後果時，他們更有能力主動預防污染。這不只是知識傳授，而是文化建設。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼微生物學訓練需要涵蓋「給藥途徑」(route of drug administration) 和「病患族群」(patient population) 的概念？

                
2. 在你的 CDMO 工廠中，是否有針對 TSE/BSE 風險的物料管理程序？這如何整合到訓練計畫中？

            

        

    

## 8.2 Personal Hygiene

    

        

## Original Text

        

The training program should explain how people and their actions are recognized as one of the greatest sources of microbiological contamination within the pharmaceutical industry. Therefore, the program should stress the requirements for maintaining a high standard of personal hygiene and how to effectively perform handwashing. The topic of hygiene should list health conditions that would restrict personnel from operating in a cleanroom.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Personal Hygiene (個人衛生)：**TR90 明確指出「人和他們的行為」是藥品產業中微生物污染的最大來源之一。訓練計畫必須涵蓋：

            

                
- 維持高標準個人衛生的要求

                
- 有效的 Handwashing (洗手) 技術

                
- 限制人員進入潔淨室的 Health Conditions (健康狀況) 清單

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

就像餐廳的廚師必須遵守嚴格的衛生標準一樣 -- 你不會希望一位感冒的廚師在開放式廚房裡為你準備壽司。同樣地，一位有傳染性疾病或皮膚傷口的操作員，在潔淨室中會成為微生物污染的活躍源頭。Health condition restrictions (健康狀況限制) 不是歧視，而是保護患者安全的必要措施。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**人是最大的污染源：**這是整個 CCS 中最重要的認知之一。一個正常的人每分鐘可以釋放數千到數百萬個微粒，而不良的衛生習慣會大幅增加這個數字。因此，個人衛生訓練不是形式，而是污染控制的第一道防線。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠中有哪些健康狀況會限制人員進入潔淨室？這份清單是否涵蓋了皮膚病、呼吸道感染、腸胃疾病等？

                
2. 洗手程序是否經過驗證？操作員是否定期接受洗手技術的評估？

            

        

    

## 8.3 Gowning

    

        

## Original Text

        

Appropriate garments and the process of gowning provides a barrier between personnel and the cleanroom and, therefore, it should be covered in detail within a training program. The program should detail observing wear and tear, use of non-shedding materials, number of uses, frequency of changes, sterilization program, etc. A description of the types and layers of garments to be worn and an explanation of how gowning prevents contamination are necessary components. Personnel assigned to execute cleaning and disinfection SOPs should regown prior to conducting aseptic operations in critical areas. Importantly, instructions for the process of gowning that would permit successful qualification of personnel in gowning should be described explicitly.

        

For detailed gowning requirements, refer to EU GMP Annex 1 Manufacture of Sterile Medicinal Products and PDA Points to Consider for Aseptic Processing: Part 1 (2015).

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Gowning (更衣)：**更衣是在人員和潔淨室之間建立物理屏障的關鍵程序。訓練計畫應詳細涵蓋：

            

                
- **Wear and Tear (磨損檢查)：**使用前檢查衣物完整性

                
- **Non-shedding Materials (不脫落材質)：**確保衣物本身不會成為微粒來源

                
- **使用次數與更換頻率：**明確規定每件衣物的使用壽命

                
- **Sterilization Program (滅菌計畫)：**衣物的滅菌週期與方法

                
- **衣物層次與類型：**不同潔淨度等級對應不同的穿著要求

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

更衣程序就像太空人穿太空衣 -- 每一個步驟都有其意義，每一層都提供特定的保護功能。如果太空衣有一個小洞，就可能危及太空人的生命。同樣地，如果潔淨室衣物有破損或穿著不當，就可能讓微生物突破這道屏障，威脅到產品和患者的安全。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**清潔消毒後需重新更衣：**TR90 特別強調，執行清潔和消毒 SOP 的人員在進行關鍵區域的無菌操作之前，必須重新更衣 (regown)。這是因為清潔消毒過程中衣物可能已被污染。

            

**資格確認導向的訓練：**更衣指導必須足夠明確，使人員能夠成功通過更衣資格確認。這意味著訓練不只是「示範」，而是要有清楚的步驟說明和評估標準。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠對更衣衣物的使用次數和洗滌/滅菌週期是否有明確規定？這些規定是否基於數據驗證？

                
2. 執行清潔消毒的人員是否在進入無菌操作前重新更衣？如果沒有，這會帶來什麼風險？

            

        

    

## 8.3.1 Gowning Qualification

    

        

## Original Text

        

Gowning qualification is the demonstration that a person is capable of consistently donning cleanroom garments and maintaining the barrier properties to ensure the exterior of the garment is not contaminated with microorganisms. Qualification should include multiple observations of the person donning the gown and taking multiple samples from the exterior of the garment after gowning to demonstrate the presence or absence of any microorganisms. Sample sites of the gown should be determined by a risk assessment that considers the specific operation. A documented rationale should explain the acceptance criteria for the personnel gowning qualification process. Personnel are prohibited from Grade A and Grade B cleanroom entry without having successfully completed gowning qualification.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Gowning Qualification (更衣資格確認)：**這是一項正式的評估程序，用以證明人員能夠一致地、正確地穿戴潔淨室衣物並維持其屏障特性。關鍵要素包括：

            

                
- **Multiple Observations (多次觀察)：**不是一次就通過，需要多次觀察確認一致性

                
- **Multiple Samples (多點取樣)：**從衣物外表面多個位置取樣進行微生物檢測

                
- **Risk Assessment (風險評估)：**取樣位置應基於特定操作的風險評估來決定

                
- **Acceptance Criteria (接受標準)：**必須有書面記錄的合格標準及其理由

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Grade A 和 Grade B 的強制要求：**TR90 明確規定，未成功完成更衣資格確認的人員「禁止」進入 Grade A 和 Grade B 潔淨室。這是一項不可妥協的要求。

            

**取樣位置的科學依據：**並非隨機取樣，而是根據風險評估決定。例如，前臂和胸部通常是高風險區域，因為它們最接近產品和關鍵操作面。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

更衣資格確認就像飛行員的技能檢定 -- 你不能只看一次降落就認定飛行員合格。考官需要多次觀察不同條件下的表現，確認其操作的一致性和可靠性。同樣地，更衣的一致性才是真正的品質保證 -- 一個人在壓力下、趕時間時是否仍然能正確更衣，這才是資格確認要驗證的能力。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠更衣資格確認要求多少次連續成功的觀察？取樣位置是否基於書面的風險評估？

                
2. 如果一位資深操作員在更衣資格確認中失敗，你的程序中是否有明確的處置流程？

            

        

    

## 8.3.2 Gowning Disqualification and Requalification

    

        

## Original Text

        

A documented program should also be established to provide the criteria that disqualifies personnel from cleanroom entry based on insufficient gowning technique and/or exceeding established microbial counts and/or trends from personnel monitoring. A matrix approach should be considered in developing the plan for disqualification, such as multiple alert-level excursions in a prescribed period, multiple action-level deviations in a prescribed period, or a combination of both. Operators can also be disqualified for observation of poor aseptic/cleanroom behavior.

        

If disqualified, a return to accessing cleanrooms would be contingent upon appropriate corrective actions being taken and successful completion of qualification (see Section 8.3.1). Additionally, requalification of gowning should be performed routinely on an annual basis or return from a long leave / extended absence for personnel to demonstrate their continued capability in gowning.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Disqualification (取消資格)：**當人員的更衣技術不足或超出微生物計數標準時，應取消其潔淨室准入資格。TR90 建議使用 Matrix Approach (矩陣方法) 來建立取消資格的標準，例如：

            

                
- 在特定期間內多次 Alert-level Excursions (警戒值偏離)

                
- 在特定期間內多次 Action-level Deviations (行動值偏差)

                
- 上述兩者的組合

                
- 觀察到不良的無菌/潔淨室行為

            

            

**Requalification (重新確認)：**應定期（年度）執行，或在人員長假/長時間缺勤後執行。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

這就像駕照的扣點制度 -- 不是一次違規就吊銷駕照，而是根據違規的嚴重程度和頻率來做累計判斷。Alert-level 就像輕微違規扣 1 點，Action-level 就像嚴重違規扣 3 點。當累計到一定程度，就暫時「吊銷」潔淨室准入資格，必須重新訓練和考核後才能恢復。年度重新確認則像定期體檢 -- 即使沒有問題，也需要定期確認能力是否維持。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**矩陣方法的優勢：**使用矩陣方法可以避免「一刀切」的判斷 -- 單次偏離可能是偶發事件，但短期內多次偏離則可能反映系統性問題。這種分層次的評估方式更加科學合理。

            

**恢復資格的前提：**取消資格後，人員必須 (1) 採取適當的矯正措施，且 (2) 成功完成資格確認，才能恢復潔淨室准入權。兩個條件缺一不可。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 工廠中，由於人員流動性較高，建議建立一套電子化的人員資格追蹤系統，自動整合環境監控數據和人員監控結果。當觸發取消資格標準時，系統自動鎖定門禁權限並通知相關主管。這樣可以確保即時反應，避免人為疏忽導致未合格人員進入潔淨室。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠目前使用矩陣方法來評估人員取消資格嗎？矩陣中包含哪些觸發條件？

                
2. 年度重新確認的執行率是否達到 100%？對於因排班或其他原因錯過年度確認的人員，如何處理？

            

        

    

## 8.4 Cleanroom Behavior

    

        

## Original Text

        

To successfully prevent contamination in manufacturing areas, it is critical for operators to always observe appropriate cleanroom behaviors, including, but not limited to, the list below. It should be noted that these behaviors apply even when using barrier technologies:

        

            
- **Move carefully:** Moving slowly and deliberately will prevent unnecessary air turbulence in a critical area thus minimizing the risk of particle-generation or shedding. The principle of slow, careful movement should be followed throughout the cleanroom, including awareness of engineering controls and locations of air returns.

            
- **Minimize conversation:** Speaking should only occur when necessary and never in a critical area.

            
- **Maintain unidirectional airflow ("first air"):** Unidirectional airflow is designed to protect sterile equipment surfaces, container-closures, and product. Disruption of the path of unidirectional flow air in the critical area can pose a risk to product sterility.

            
- **Perform interventions carefully:** Using the correct tools and equipment and performing interventions in a manner that does not compromise sterility of the product ensures that unidirectional airflow over sterile product and sterile components will not be interrupted. When using a restricted access barrier system (RABS) system, barrier doors should be opened only when necessary and for the shortest time possible.

            
- **Position body:** Keeping the entire body out of the path of the unidirectional airflow will prevent airflow from being blocked over critical surfaces. Personnel should not reach across open containers, exposed product, or components and product contact parts/surfaces.

            
- **Maintain proper gown control:** Prior to and throughout aseptic operations, operators should not engage in any activity that poses an unreasonable contamination risk to the gown, such as unnecessary contact with walls, floors, and cleaned surfaces. After initial gowning, sterile gloves should be regularly sanitized or changed, as appropriate, to minimize the risk of contamination. If damage (e.g., hole, tear) is detected when donning the gown, the gown should be replaced immediately. If damage is detected during manufacturing, the operator should exit the cleanroom and regown.

            
- **Protect sterile parts:** Parts should be staged and grouped for setup to allow for consistent setup order—from top to bottom, back to front—for the protection of all sterile parts. During setup, sterile product contact parts should remain protected until setup is completed. Between uses, sterile tools should be held under Grade A conditions and maintained in a manner that prevents contamination (e.g., placed in sterilized containers) or should be replaced. Parts should be sterilized together, whenever possible, to minimize aseptic connections during setup.

            
- **Minimize surface contact:** Personnel should not come in direct contact with sterile product, containers, closures, or critical surfaces with any part of their gowns or gloves. Sterile tools should always be used, where possible.

            
- **Manage gloves:** Regular glove sanitization techniques and frequency and re-gloving activities should always be followed. At a minimum, single gloves should be worn in supporting areas; sterile double-gloves should be worn in all conventional aseptic processing areas. A fresh pair of sterile gloves should be worn upon each entry to Grade A clean room. Gloves should be checked for integrity upon donning and prior to performing an intervention. If damage (e.g., hole, tear) is detected when donning the glove, the glove should immediately be replaced. If damage is detected during manufacturing, the operator should follow an established risk-based procedure to replace the glove while limiting any contamination hazard to the operation.

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Cleanroom Behavior (潔淨室行為規範)：**TR90 列出九大行為準則，每一項都直接關係到污染風險的控制。特別注意：這些行為要求即使在使用 Barrier Technologies (屏障技術，如 RABS 或 Isolator) 時也同樣適用。

            

核心原則可歸納為三大類：

            

                
- **氣流保護：**謹慎移動、維持 First Air (初始空氣)、正確身體定位

                
- **屏障維護：**管控更衣、管理手套、最小化表面接觸

                
- **無菌保護：**謹慎介入操作、保護無菌部件、最小化對話

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像你在一個佈滿蜘蛛絲的房間裡行走 -- 每一個動作都必須緩慢而刻意，因為任何突然的動作都會擾動空氣，破壞那些脆弱的結構。在潔淨室中，你要保護的不是蜘蛛絲，而是單向氣流 (unidirectional airflow) 形成的「無菌空氣幕」。任何不必要的動作、說話、或不當的身體定位，都可能破壞這道保護屏障。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**First Air (初始空氣) 原則：**這是無菌操作中最重要的概念之一 -- 從 HEPA 過濾器流出的空氣在接觸產品之前，不應接觸任何其他表面或障礙物。操作員的手、手臂或身體都不應阻擋 first air 到達關鍵表面的路徑。

            

**手套管理的層次要求：**

            

                
- 支援區域：最低要求單層手套

                
- 傳統無菌加工區域：無菌雙層手套

                
- 每次進入 Grade A：更換全新的無菌手套

            

            

**組裝順序原則：**從上到下、從後到前 (top to bottom, back to front)，確保已組裝的無菌部件不會被後續操作污染。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 工廠中，由於操作員可能需要在不同產品線之間輪換，建議為每條產線製作一份「潔淨室行為速查卡」，標示該產線特定的氣流方向、空氣回風口位置、以及關鍵介入操作的正確姿勢。搭配定期的視頻回放訓練，讓操作員能「看到自己的動作」並自我改善。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠是否有明確記錄每個操作工位的 first air 方向和氣流路徑？操作員是否能準確指出這些位置？

                
2. RABS 門板的開啟時間是否有監控和記錄？如何確保「僅在必要時開啟且時間最短」？

                
3. 當手套在操作中發現破損時，你的風險評估程序是否涵蓋對已加工產品的影響評估？

            

        

    

## 8.4.1 Aseptic Operator Training and Qualification

    

        

## Original Text

        

Aseptic processing depends on personnel operating in a manner that does not disturb airflow, minimizes the generation of particles, and does not introduce bioburden into the process through inappropriate handling of product contact equipment or components. Aseptic operator trainees should only be permitted to perform interventions upon successful participation with a process simulation. Participation in the process simulation requires that the operator perform a pre-identified set or subset of critical tasks that they would perform during batch production, and the result of the process simulation was successful. Where there are practical limitations or an aseptic process simulation is not required, operators can be qualified outside of an aseptic process simulation provided the qualification exercise is representative of worst-case process conditions.

        

After an operator has been initially qualified, the facility should schedule an annual refresher training program as well as participation in routine aseptic process simulation (i.e., media-fill study). Access to the aseptic processing area should be controlled (e.g., badge access, etc.) and a procedure should be established for disqualification and timely revocation of access.

        

Disqualification should result in retraining and requalification, reassignment, or permanent removal from the cleanroom. Personnel would be considered disqualified from performing in an aseptic filling process if they had participated in a media-fill study that resulted in the detection of positive (failing) units and the root cause is determined to be inappropriate aseptic behavior. Additionally, disqualification should be considered if personnel participate in a commercial production lot that does not meet the requirements for sterility testing and the root cause is determined to be inappropriate aseptic behavior.

        

In addition to training and qualification/disqualification, there should be regular oversight of personnel following established, written procedures and performing good cleanroom behaviors and aseptic technique during manufacturing operations. Routine oversight through an observation program of aseptic operators should form part of the aseptic-operator training and qualification.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Aseptic Operator Training and Qualification (無菌操作員訓練與資格確認)：**這是比一般潔淨室人員更高層級的要求。關鍵要素：

            

                
- **Process Simulation (製程模擬)：**操作員必須在培養基充填試驗 (media-fill study) 中成功執行其預定的關鍵任務，才能獲得資格

                
- **Worst-case Process Conditions (最壞情況製程條件)：**當無法進行製程模擬時，資格確認練習必須代表最壞情況

                
- **Annual Refresher (年度複訓)：**初始合格後需定期參加複訓和例行培養基充填

                
- **Access Control (准入控制)：**使用門禁卡等方式控制無菌加工區域的進入

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**取消資格的觸發條件：**

            

                
- 參與的培養基充填試驗檢出陽性（不合格）單元，且根因為不當的無菌行為

                
- 參與的商業生產批次未通過無菌試驗，且根因為不當的無菌行為

            

            

**取消資格後的處置選項：**

            

                
- 重新訓練和重新確認

                
- 重新分配至其他崗位

                
- 永久移除潔淨室准入權

            

            

注意：取消資格不是懲罰性的，而是風險管理的必要手段。重點在於根因分析和矯正措施。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

無菌操作員的資格確認就像外科醫師的考核 -- 你不能僅靠讀書和考試就上手術台，必須先在模擬手術中成功執行操作。Media-fill study 就是無菌操作員的「模擬手術」。如果在模擬中出現問題（長出微生物），那就意味著實際操作中也可能污染產品。年度的複訓和 media-fill 參與，則確保操作員的技能不會隨時間退化。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 環境中，Media-fill study 的排程是一項挑戰，因為每位操作員都需要參與，同時又不能影響商業生產排程。建議做法：

            

                
- 建立「資格確認日曆」，提前 6 個月規劃所有人員的 media-fill 參與排程

                
- 利用產品轉換或年度停機期間安排 media-fill

                
- 確保每位操作員在 media-fill 中執行的任務與其日常工作完全一致

                
- 將門禁系統與資格確認資料庫連結，過期的資格自動鎖定准入

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠是否要求所有無菌操作員每年參與 media-fill？如果操作員因排班原因錯過，如何處理？

                
2. 當 media-fill 失敗時，你的根因調查程序是否能有效區分「操作員行為問題」和「設備/環境問題」？

                
3. 操作員的門禁權限是否與資格確認狀態即時連動？

            

        

    

## 8.4.2 Aseptic Observer Program

    

        

## Original Text

        

An aseptic-observer program is a structured process through which aseptic operators are trained to routinely assess and evaluate one another's performance and compliance to all aspects of training and qualification, especially with respect to cleanroom behaviors and aseptic practices. The aseptic-observer program not only identifies areas for improvement but also reinforces observed best practices. An aseptic-observer program can follow the seven simple steps illustrated in Figure 8.4.2-1.

        

### Figure 8.4.2-1 — Aseptic-Operator's Observation 7-Step Program

        

**Step 1: Qualify Operators**  

        All personnel included in the aseptic-observer program should be fully qualified.

        

**Step 2: Identify and Train Aseptic Observers**  

        Aseptic-behavior observers are trained individuals with experience in aseptic behaviors and practices who are respected by the operators.

        

**Step 3: Observe Aseptic Behaviors**  

        Observers use a defined expectations list of behaviors as described in Section 8.4. Behaviors and interventions performed during manufacturing should be consistent with interventions qualified during aseptic process simulations.

        

**Step 4: Report and Provide Feedback**  

        Observers should immediately give feedback to operators on their behaviors as part of continuous improvement. Observations discussed with personnel and frontline management should include overall observations, identification of any observation trends, and potential corrective actions. Potential corrective actions might include refresher training, procedural revisions for clarification, equipment modifications, or use of tools.

        

**Step 5: Improve Aseptic Processes and Behaviors**  

        Barriers to improvement (e.g., process/line configuration, material availability, procedure) should be addressed, and corrective actions should be identified and implemented.

        

**Step 6: Analyze and Trend Observations**  

        Periodically, long-term trending should be performed to determine root cause and to proactively address the most frequent observations. Trend results should then be communicated to operators, management, and support personnel according to site practices. An overall risk assessment tool may also be used for this purpose.

        

**Step 7: Maintain Program**  

        Periodically, the observation program itself should be reviewed to determine if changes are needed to adapt to personnel, facility, and/or process changes. Modifications may include updates to the defined expectations list of behaviors (see Step #3), communication of results, data trending, or effectiveness of corrective actions.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Aseptic Observer Program (無菌觀察員計畫)：**這是一種結構化的同儕評估程序，讓經過訓練的無菌操作員定期評估彼此的表現和合規性。這個計畫有雙重目的：

            

                
- 識別需要改善的領域

                
- 強化觀察到的最佳實踐

            

            

七步驟循環構成了一個完整的 PDCA (Plan-Do-Check-Act) 改善迴路。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**七步驟計畫的核心邏輯：**

            

                
- **Step 1-2 (建立基礎)：**確保參與者和觀察員都是合格且受尊重的

                
- **Step 3-4 (觀察與回饋)：**使用標準化的行為期望清單進行觀察，並即時給予回饋

                
- **Step 5-6 (改善與趨勢)：**消除改善障礙，進行長期趨勢分析以發現系統性問題

                
- **Step 7 (維護計畫)：**定期檢視計畫本身的有效性並調整

            

            

**關鍵成功因素：**觀察員必須是「受操作員尊重的人」(respected by the operators)。如果觀察員被視為「監視者」而非「同儕教練」，計畫將失去其文化建設的價值。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

無菌觀察員計畫就像運動隊伍中的「影片回顧」(film review) -- 教練和隊員一起觀看比賽錄影，不是為了指責誰犯了錯，而是為了識別可以改善的地方並強化好的表現。最好的球隊不僅有好的球員，更有持續互相學習和改善的文化。同樣地，最好的無菌操作團隊不僅有合格的個人，更有持續觀察、回饋和改善的機制。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

建立有效的無菌觀察員計畫的實務建議：

            

                
- **數位化觀察表單：**使用平板電腦上的電子表單取代紙本記錄，方便即時輸入和後續趨勢分析

                
- **積極正面的回饋文化：**觀察報告不僅記錄偏差，也記錄良好實踐，建立正向激勵

                
- **與環境監控數據交叉分析：**將觀察員報告與環境監控數據結合，識別人員行為與環境數據之間的關聯性

                
- **季度趨勢報告：**每季度彙整觀察數據，向管理層和操作團隊報告主要發現和改善進度

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠目前是否有正式的無菌觀察員計畫？如果有，觀察頻率和覆蓋率如何？

                
2. 觀察員的選拔標準是什麼？是否確保他們「受操作員尊重」？

                
3. 觀察結果是否定期進行趨勢分析？最常見的偏差類型是什麼？這些偏差是否與環境監控數據有相關性？

            

        

    

    

### 本節重點回顧 Section Summary

    

        
- **人員是最大污染源：**TR90 反覆強調人員及其行為是藥品製造中微生物污染的最大來源，因此人員訓練與資格確認是 CCS 的核心要素。

        
- **六大必修課程：**基礎微生物學、人員流向、物料與廢棄物流向、環境控制、清潔與消毒、製程設計 -- 這是所有製造人員進入產區前的最低訓練要求。

        
- **四大核心主題：**基礎微生物學、個人衛生、更衣、潔淨室行為 -- 這四項構成了污染控制訓練計畫的骨幹。

        
- **更衣的完整生命週期管理：**從資格確認 (multiple observations + multiple samples) 到取消資格 (matrix approach) 再到重新確認 (annual basis)，形成閉環管理。

        
- **九大潔淨室行為準則：**謹慎移動、最小化對話、維持 first air、謹慎介入、正確身體定位、管控更衣、保護無菌部件、最小化表面接觸、管理手套。

        
- **無菌操作員的進階要求：**必須在 media-fill 中成功執行關鍵任務才能獲得資格，年度複訓和 media-fill 參與為持續要求。

        
- **無菌觀察員計畫的七步驟：**從操作員資格確認到觀察、回饋、改善、趨勢分析，再到計畫本身的維護，形成持續改善的閉環。

        
- **從「非全面性」到「全面性」思維轉變：**不再認為「遵循 SOP 就夠了」，而是追求理解危害、品質文化建設和持續改善的全面性方法。

## Section 7: Equipment Design 設備設計 (p30-p34)

# Section 9.0 Equipment Design, Validation, and Ongoing Control

    

設備設計、確效與持續管控

    

PDA Technical Report No. 90 — Contamination Control Strategy | p30 - p34

    

### 本章學習目標

    

        
- 理解設備設計如何作為 Contamination Control Strategy (CCS) 污染控制策略的核心要素，並掌握「整體性方法 (Holistic Approach)」的思維模式

        
- 掌握設備設計階段應考量的關鍵項目清單，包括封閉系統、衛生級設計、屏障技術與互鎖機制

        
- 認識 Cleaning Validation (清潔確效) 的侷限性，特別是 Biofilm (生物膜) 對清潔效果的長期影響

        
- 學習設備持續管控階段的查核要點，包括清潔狀態識別、無菌保持時間、RABS 門開啟管理

        
- 了解 Single-Use Systems (一次性使用系統)、Barrier Technology (屏障技術)、Product Pathway (產品路徑) 的特殊考量

        
- 掌握設備維護 (Maintenance) 在 CCS 中的角色，包括預防性維護計畫、Temporary Gray Space Enclosure (TGSE) 的管控策略

    

    

### 本節目錄

    

        9.0 總論
        9.1 設備設計
        9.2 清潔確效
        9.3 持續管控
        9.4 特殊考量
        9.4.1 一次性使用
        9.4.2 屏障技術
        9.4.3 產品路徑
        9.5 維護
    

9.0 Equipment Design, Validation, and Ongoing Control

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

For the CCS, equipment design, validation, and ongoing control considerations should all be developed with the goal of reducing the risk of contamination (Section 15.0, Table 1, Table 3, and Table 4). To be effective, these elements should be built in a holistic manner, that is, all the elements should work together as interwoven and successively linked events with the common goal of preventing contamination. Table 9.0-1 outlines a holistic approach to equipment considerations.

        

            
                Table 9.0-1 Holistic Approach to Equipment Considerations
                
                    
                    
                
| Non-Holistic Approach | Holistic Approach |
| --- | --- |
                
                    
                    
                
| Nonsterile equipment is always appropriate for nonsterile processes | Design the equipment controls to prevent and reduce contamination risk under worst-case circumstances |
                
                    
                    
                
| Cleaning is validated and therefore cannot be a root cause or contributing factor for contamination | Design the equipment handling procedures with the understanding that validated cleaning practices can be overchallenged by poor equipment hold practices; nonsterile equipment with any residual moisture will foul with biofilm over time |
                
                    
                    
                
| Perform only testing after a clean hold time is exceeded but do not reclean | Perform full cleaning after a clean hold time is exceeded to reduce any build-up of biofilm, which can be more difficult to remove later |
            

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Holistic Approach (整體性方法)：**TR90 在此強調設備管控不是一個個獨立的檢查點，而是「設計 → 確效 → 日常管控」三者如同鏈條般環環相扣。任何一個環節的疏忽，都可能讓其他環節的努力功虧一簣。

            

**CCS 中的設備角色：**設備是 CCS 架構中「硬體防線」的核心。與人員管控 (Section 8.0)、環境管控 (Section 7.0) 並列為三大支柱。設備設計得好，可以大幅降低對人員操作和環境控制的依賴。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像蓋一棟醫院：「非整體性方法」就像只關心手術室的無菌，卻忽略了從大門到手術室的走廊、電梯、空調是否也做好了感染管控。「整體性方法」則是從建築設計階段就規劃好動線、空氣流向、清潔區域劃分，讓每個環節都互相支援，不留死角。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Table 9.0-1 的核心訊息：**「清潔已確效」不代表萬事大吉。確效只是在特定條件下驗證了清潔程序的有效性，但實際操作中的 hold time 超標、殘留水分等情境，都可能讓已確效的清潔程序失效。Biofilm (生物膜) 一旦形成，移除難度將大幅增加。

            

這正是 EU GMP Annex 1 (2022) 的精神：不能僅依賴驗證結果，必須以風險為導向持續監控。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 在你的工廠中，設備清潔確效後是否曾因 hold time 超標而直接放行？這樣做的風險是什麼？

                
2. 請試著列出你工廠中一個「非整體性」的設備管控案例，並思考如何改善為「整體性」方法。

            

        

    

9.1 Equipment Design

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Process contamination risks that are not controlled by equipment design may result in additional risks that need to be mitigated by other controls, such as creation of procedures, use of sterile tools, segregation, or shorter hold times. Not putting these other controls in place could lead to higher operational costs and higher risk for the life of the product.

        

For example, if the decision is made during process development to leave an in-process step as manual and open, all the surrounding control elements, including the personnel controls and all environmental controls (e.g., cleaning, gowning, flow), should be intensively built up to prevent contamination. In addition, more quality control testing/monitoring will be required at that step, and EM will need to be done every time that step is performed. The CCS should be reevaluated for risk mitigation from development to commercial phase to improve the controls as manufacturing scales up.

        

Items to be considered during the equipment design phase of CCS include:

        

            
- Equipment is a closed system wherever possible

            
- Equipment is for sanitary use (e.g., 316SS versus a lower grade of stainless steel, avoid any parts that may generate particles)

            
- Fixed probes (e.g., for active viable air and total airborne particle sampling in an isolator) locations determined by an EM risk assessment and airflow visualization studies

            
- Surfaces are smooth and easy to clean

            
- Equipment is designed to minimize routine human intervention in critical areas

            
- Barrier equipment designed with interlocks to prevent operator mistakes and/or alert operator about component malfunction

            
- Ease of access and compatibility with operator access (in isolator or RABS) during aseptic assembly, as well as when performing interventions, to prevent operators leaning over open product or components

            
- Parts are designed to be sterilized as a unit to minimize connections during setup

            
- Sterile pathways covered during setup, removing covers only at the end

            
- Mechanical and electrical adjustments designed to be made outside the aseptic processing area

            
- Are plans for pipes, ducts, and other utilities to be installed designed to not create recesses or have unsealed openings and/or surfaces that are difficult to clean?

            
- Through-the-wall passages for pipes and tubing sealed or gasketed, with no openings that expose wall interiors

            
- All designs result in slopes for drainage

            
- Exhaust filters allow exhaust to meet area classification where it is being discharged (e.g., Grade A or B)

            
- Source air for air-break filters on autoclaves or lyophilizers drawn from the cleanroom rather than from the plant area

            
- Electronics are covered or provided with a wipeable surface that is resistant to disinfectants (e.g., equipment computers or keyboards)

            
- Equipment can be easily protected during storage

            
- Ways to measure alert/action alarm conditions for all critical operating parameters

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**設計決定成本 (Design Drives Cost)：**TR90 開宗明義指出，如果設備設計階段未能有效控制污染風險，後續就必須用更多的 SOP、無菌工具、區隔措施和更短的 hold time 來彌補。這些補救措施不僅增加營運成本，也增加了產品生命週期內的風險。

            

**Closed System (封閉系統)：**設備盡可能設計為封閉系統是首要原則。封閉系統意味著產品不會暴露於外部環境，從源頭消除了微生物和粒子污染的風險。

            

**Interlock (互鎖機制)：**屏障設備上的互鎖裝置可以防止操作員犯錯（如在不當時機開門）或警告設備元件故障。這是「設備防呆」的具體體現。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

設備設計就像蓋房子的地基和結構。如果地基沒打好（設備設計不佳），後續就得不斷加裝警報系統、安排更多保全（更多 SOP、更多監控），但房子還是不穩。反之，地基穩固的房子（良好的設備設計），後續維護簡單、住起來安心。在製藥業，這個差異可能意味著每批次數十萬到數百萬的成本差異。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Manual and Open 的代價：**如果某個製程步驟選擇了「手動且開放」的設計，TR90 明確指出必須「全面強化」周圍的所有管控措施。這包括：

            

                
- 加強人員管控（更嚴格的更衣、行為規範）

                
- 加強環境管控（更高等級的清潔、氣流管理）

                
- 增加品質測試/監控頻率

                
- 每次執行該步驟都必須進行 EM (Environmental Monitoring，環境監測)

            

            

從開發階段到商業化階段，CCS 都應持續重新評估以改善管控。

        

        

            

#### 設計查核清單重點歸納

            

TR90 列出的 18 項設計考量可歸納為四大原則：

            

                
- **隔離原則：**封閉系統、屏障設備、互鎖機制、減少人員介入

                
- **可清潔原則：**光滑表面、衛生級材料 (316SS)、排水坡度、密封貫穿口

                
- **可監控原則：**固定探頭位置、Alert/Action 警報條件、電子設備可擦拭

                
- **可維護原則：**機械/電氣調整在無菌區外進行、設備可輕鬆保護儲存

            

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 場景：**你的 CDMO 正在評估引進新的充填線。客戶要求的產品需要一個開放式手動加料步驟。根據 TR90 的指導，你應該：

            

                
1. 首先評估是否可以改為封閉系統設計來消除此步驟

                
2. 如果無法避免，應計算「全面強化管控」的額外成本（人員、EM、QC 測試）

                
3. 將此成本回饋給客戶的報價，或建議客戶投資封閉系統以降低長期營運成本

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的充填線上，autoclaves 的 air-break filter 進氣來源是潔淨室還是廠房區域？如果來自廠房區域，風險是什麼？

                
2. 列出三個你的設備上「不符合」TR90 設計清單要求的項目，並提出改善建議。

                
3. 為什麼 TR90 要求「零件應設計為可作為一個單元滅菌」而非在現場逐一連接？

            

        

    

9.2 Equipment Cleaning Validation

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Cleaning validation is essential, but it is also limited in its value to predict microbial control over the lifespan of equipment due to the timing and amount of validation testing and the limitations of traditional microbiological testing. Historically, cleaning validation has primarily focused on the removal of product residue and less on prevention of biofilms. Additionally, sampling techniques and culture-based microbiological testing are known to have limited detection power for a range of microorganisms.

        

Equipment validation is often performed on new equipment that has not been exposed to the broad range of factors that can reduce the effectiveness of cleaning. Existing equipment is revalidated on a defined schedule and/or if the validated conditions are no longer relevant (e.g., new product introduction, new equipment configuration). Factors that reduce the effectiveness of a cleaning procedure include biofilm-producing organisms, years of residue build-up, normal wear, and surface damage.

        

Some cleaning regimens can be effective for years until a worst-case biofilm-forming organism is introduced, for example, Arthrobacter russicus, which can develop a biofilm that is difficult to remove in a low-nutrient environment in as little as three days. PDA Technical Report 69 provides a thorough guideline on biofilm prevention, including scenarios of contamination from equipment. Practical considerations for equipment cleaning are presented in Section 15.0, Table 8. For further information on cleaning validation, refer to PDA Technical Report 29 and PDA Technical Report 49.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Cleaning Validation (清潔確效) 的侷限性：**TR90 在此提出了一個很重要但常被忽視的觀點 — 清潔確效是必要的，但其預測設備整個使用壽命內微生物控制效果的能力是有限的。原因包括：

            

                
- 確效時機和測試量有限（通常只做 3 批）

                
- 傳統微生物測試方法的偵測能力有限

                
- 確效通常在新設備上進行，未接觸到長期使用的各種劣化因素

            

            

**Biofilm (生物膜)：**微生物在設備表面形成的保護性群落結構。一旦形成，其對清潔劑和消毒劑的抵抗力會大幅增強，使常規清潔程序失效。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

清潔確效就像汽車的新車出廠檢測 — 新車時一切指標都完美，但你不能因此就認為這輛車永遠不需要保養。隨著使用年限增加，引擎積碳 (= residue build-up)、橡膠老化 (= surface damage)、甚至遇到特殊路況 (= worst-case biofilm organism) 都可能讓原本有效的保養程序不再足夠。Biofilm 就像水管裡的水垢 — 一旦形成就很難徹底清除，而且會越積越厚。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Arthrobacter russicus 案例：**TR90 特別點名這個微生物，它能在低營養環境中僅三天就形成難以去除的 biofilm。這個案例說明：

            

                
- 你的清潔程序可能有效運行多年，直到遇到一個 worst-case 的 biofilm 形成菌

                
- 不能因為「從未出過問題」就認為清潔程序永遠足夠

                
- Clean hold time 的管控至關重要 — 任何殘留水分都可能成為 biofilm 的溫床

            

            

**交叉參考：**PDA TR69 (biofilm 預防)、PDA TR29 和 TR49 (清潔確效) 提供了更詳細的指引。

        

        

            

#### 影響清潔有效性的因素矩陣

            

```

清潔有效性下降因素：
  1. Biofilm-producing organisms (生物膜生成菌)
  2. Years of residue build-up (多年殘留物累積)
  3. Normal wear (正常磨損)
  4. Surface damage (表面損傷)

風險公式概念：
  實際清潔風險 = f(設備使用年限, 產品殘留特性,
                    微生物種類, 表面狀態, hold time 管控)

  確效結論有效性 ∝ 1 / (設備年齡 + 累積使用次數)
            
```

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠是否有針對設備表面狀態進行定期視覺檢查的 SOP？如果設備使用超過 5 年，你會如何調整清潔確效策略？

                
2. 假設你的環境監測發現了 Arthrobacter 屬微生物，你應該啟動哪些調查和因應措施？

                
3. 傳統清潔確效主要聚焦於產品殘留物去除，請說明為什麼這不足以預防 biofilm 形成。

            

        

    

9.3 Equipment Ongoing Control

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

While equipment can be well designed and validated, routine and ongoing control of equipment during use is also an important consideration in the CCS strategy. Equipment that is not controlled effectively can contaminate the product, harbor biofilms of microorganisms and act as a reservoir for microbial contamination, which can be directly introduced into the process stream.

        

Contamination control considerations for the control phase include:

        

            
- Prior to use, are processing vessels and components cleaned and sanitized? How is the clean status of equipment identified and verified? Is the cleaning/sanitization status readily identified with labels/tags on each piece of equipment? How do operators know the clean hold time of the equipment?

            
- Are sterilized holding tanks and any contained liquids held under positive pressure or appropriately sealed to prevent microbial contamination?

            
- Is sterilized equipment discarded or removed from the area when the packaging or cover is not integral, as evidenced by holes, rips, or tears or when unexpected condensate is present? Do site procedures for aseptic filling-line setup include a check for the presence of wet components and state that these should not be used?

            
- Is the equipment included in the preventive maintenance program? Does the program include elastomer management and replacement?

            
- Has the time interval between the washing, drying, and sterilization of components, containers, and equipment been qualified, as well as the time interval between their sterilization and use?

            
- Is the equipment visually confirmed to be dry prior to wrapping or covering?

            
- Are appropriate protective coverings applied to items for sterilization/depyrogenation so that sterility is maintained post-sterilization?

            
- Is sterilized equipment clearly differentiated from nonsterilized items (e.g., color-change indicator)?

            
- Are presterilized materials that cannot be sterilized via passage into the Grade A space (e.g., via double-door autoclave, dry heat oven) double-wrapped, at a minimum, allowing layer removal when transferred into the clean areas? Are sterile surfaces exposed only in the critical area?

            
- Is dirty equipment removed as soon as possible and cleaned within the dirty equipment hold time?

            
- Are doors to RABS open only when necessary and for the shortest duration? Is there a validated recovery time set for airflows?

            
- Is there a transfer plan in place to ensure equipment storage does not result in the introduction of contamination when returning it to the manufacturing area?

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Reservoir for Microbial Contamination (微生物污染儲存庫)：**設備如果管控不善，不僅會成為一次性的污染源，更會成為持續性的微生物「巢穴」。Biofilm 一旦在設備內壁或管路中形成，就會持續釋放微生物進入製程流中，成為反覆出現的污染根源。

            

**Clean Hold Time vs. Dirty Hold Time：**

            

                
- **Clean Hold Time (潔淨保持時間)：**設備清潔/滅菌後到使用前的最大允許放置時間

                
- **Dirty Hold Time (髒污保持時間)：**設備使用完畢後到開始清潔前的最大允許放置時間

            

            

兩者都必須經過確效，因為超過任何一個時間限制都可能導致微生物增殖或 biofilm 形成。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

設備的持續管控就像家裡的冰箱管理：

            

                
- **Clean hold time** = 食物的保存期限標籤（過期就不能用）

                
- **Dirty hold time** = 碗盤不能放在水槽太久不洗（會長黴菌）

                
- **Status label** = 冰箱裡食物的日期標籤（清楚標示狀態）

                
- **Unexpected condensate** = 食物包裝出現水滴（可能已經變質）

                
- **Color-change indicator** = 雞蛋的新鮮度檢測器（一眼就知道狀態）

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**12 項查核要點可歸納為五大管控領域：**

            

                
- **狀態管控：**清潔/滅菌狀態標示、有色變色指示劑、目視確認乾燥

                
- **時間管控：**Clean hold time、Dirty hold time、滅菌到使用的時間間隔

                
- **完整性管控：**包裝破損即棄、預滅菌物料雙層包裝、RABS 門開啟控制

                
- **正壓管控：**已滅菌儲槽維持正壓或密封

                
- **轉運管控：**設備儲存與返回製造區的轉運計畫

            

        

        

            

#### RABS 門開啟管控

            

TR90 特別提到 RABS 門只能在必要時開啟，且持續時間應盡可能短，並且需要有經過確效的氣流 **Recovery Time (恢復時間)**。這意味著每次開門後，都需要等待氣流恢復到合格狀態。這是 EU GMP Annex 1 對 RABS 操作的核心要求之一。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 場景：**你的工廠剛完成一批充填，下一批需要等待 16 小時後才開始。操作員在收工時清潔了設備並貼上「已清潔」標籤。根據 TR90 的管控要求，你應確保：

            

                
1. 「已清潔」標籤上包含清潔日期/時間，操作員可以對照 Clean hold time

                
2. 設備在包裝/覆蓋前已視覺確認乾燥

                
3. 如果 Clean hold time 在下一批開始前會超標，應重新清潔/滅菌

                
4. 設備儲存區域有防止污染引入的管控措施

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠如何區分已滅菌和未滅菌的設備？除了 color-change indicator，還有哪些方法？

                
2. 如果一個已滅菌的零件包裝上發現了一個小破洞但零件看起來很乾淨，你會怎麼處理？為什麼？

                
3. 為什麼 TR90 要求「濕的零件不應使用」？水分與微生物污染之間的關係是什麼？

            

        

    

9.4 Special Equipment Considerations

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Section 15.0, Table 1 provides a concise overview of the items discussed in Section 9.4.

        
        

### 9.4.1 Use of Single-Use Equipment

        

Single-use bags and product flow paths are increasingly being incorporated into manufacturing processes because they can provide a closed-system manufacturing environment. For example, they can be used for raw materials and sterile drug substance and as part of the sterile filtration process to drug product. These systems may be irradiated and designed to allow processing to occur without exposure to the external environment. Checking the sterilization cycles for this equipment upon receipt is very important (10). Observations for leaks or holes before and during use is very important. These systems are often linked with tube welders to connect different single-use systems (SUS) without breaching the sterile product pathway. It is essential the welders are used properly with the correct technique and maintenance (correct blades, wafers, etc. changed at appropriate intervals) and welds inspected prior to use. The risk to the process from this equipment is that leak/integrity testing often cannot be performed prior to and after use. Therefore, vendors for this equipment work to develop such safeguards to reduce these risks. More information on SUS can be found in PDA Technical Report No. 66: Application of Single-Use Systems in Pharmaceutical Manufacturing.

        

Single-use rapid-transfer ports can be used to dock isolators for the transfer of sterile materials. For example, stoppers may be sterilized directly into these single-use containers and subsequently transferred into a Grade A isolator.

        
        

### 9.4.2 Use of Barrier Technology

        

Barrier separation technology is preferred for use in a CCS for operations that are not fully closed, as it is increasingly important to separate the operator from the process. The use of isolators and RABS units support this practice, as interventions occur using special RABS or isolator gloves integrated within the system. The design of such equipment is important; for instance, the gloves should be placed appropriately where the interventions to be performed do not require the operator to reach over sterile product or components. A glove test strategy, combining visual and physical leak tests, should be defined for isolators and RABS. Where RABS are used, the timing, frequency, and duration of door-openings are restricted to limit risk of contamination.

        
        

### 9.4.3 Product Pathways

        

The product pathway is the environment in which the product is exposed within the system; it may include piping, vessels, and other equipment. Assessment of the control of contamination includes a closure risk analysis of the product pathway. Closed systems offer the lowest risk. Any open steps in the product pathway should be evaluated for improvements that may reduce or eliminate the risk. This may involve the use of SUS or rapid transfer ports, sterile-to-sterile connections, or equipment that is designed for closed-system dispensing and sampling.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Single-Use Systems, SUS (一次性使用系統)：**SUS 的最大優勢在於提供封閉式製造環境，消除了 CIP/SIP 的需求以及交叉污染的風險。但 TR90 也指出其核心風險 — 通常無法在使用前和使用後進行 leak/integrity testing。

            

**Tube Welder (管路焊接機)：**用於在不破壞無菌產品路徑的前提下連接不同的 SUS。焊接品質直接影響產品路徑的完整性，因此刀片/晶片的定期更換和焊接接頭的使用前檢查至關重要。

            

**Barrier Separation Technology (屏障隔離技術)：**對於無法完全封閉的操作，isolator (隔離器) 和 RABS (限制進出屏障系統) 是 CCS 的首選方案。核心目的是將操作員與製程分離。

            

**Product Pathway (產品路徑)：**產品在系統中暴露的環境。進行 closure risk analysis (封閉性風險分析) 是評估產品路徑污染風險的關鍵方法。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

**SUS = 免洗餐具：**就像餐廳使用免洗餐具可以消除洗碗不乾淨的風險，但你必須確保包裝是完整的（沒有破洞），而且要在使用前檢查。SUS 的挑戰在於 — 有些「包裝」你無法在使用前完全測試其密封性。

            

**Barrier Technology = 太空站的操作手套：**太空人透過太空站的專用手套箱操作危險材料，手套的位置必須設計在合理的操作角度，避免太空人必須「彎腰越過」操作對象。同樣，isolator/RABS 的手套位置設計必須避免操作員需要跨越無菌產品或零件。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**SUS 的關鍵管控點：**

            

                
- 接收時確認滅菌週期資料

                
- 使用前和使用中觀察是否有洩漏或破洞

                
- Tube welder 的正確使用技術和維護

                
- 焊接接頭在使用前必須檢查

            

            

**Glove Test Strategy (手套測試策略)：**對於 isolator 和 RABS，必須定義結合目視檢查和物理洩漏測試的手套測試策略。手套是屏障系統中最脆弱的環節，任何針孔洩漏都可能破壞無菌環境。

            

**Product Pathway 風險層級：**Closed system (最低風險) > Sterile-to-sterile connection > SUS/RTP > Open step (最高風險)。任何開放步驟都應評估是否可以改善為更低風險的選項。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 場景：**你的工廠使用 SUS 進行藥液配製，並透過 tube welder 連接到無菌過濾系統。最近發生了一次微生物偏差，調查顯示焊接接頭處有微小滲漏。你應該：

            

                
1. 立即確認 tube welder 的維護紀錄（刀片/晶片是否按時更換）

                
2. 檢討焊接操作 SOP 和操作員訓練紀錄

                
3. 評估是否增加焊接接頭的使用前目視/物理檢查頻率

                
4. 考慮與供應商合作開發使用前完整性測試方法

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠使用 isolator 還是 RABS？請比較兩者在操作彈性和污染風險方面的差異。

                
2. 在產品路徑的 closure risk analysis 中，你會如何評估一個「每批需要手動取樣」的步驟？提出至少兩個降低風險的改善方案。

                
3. 為什麼 TR90 強調 glove 的位置設計不應要求操作員跨越無菌產品？這與 Section 8.0 的人員管控有什麼關聯？

            

        

    

9.5 Maintenance

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Regular equipment maintenance is the key to preventing failures of the cleanroom environmental control systems (HVAC) and production equipment and ensuring the cleanrooms and equipment are operating in their validated state. Maintenance is a risk management practice used to maximize production and minimize loss and waste (see Section 15.0, Table 5). Section 17.0: Appendix III contains case studies of contamination related to the lack of adequate maintenance.

        

Maintenance activities can also pose contamination risks if not done correctly, starting with making appropriate design choices that reduce the amount of, or increase the ease of, maintenance based on failure mode and effects analysis (FMEA). The best design practice is to build a gray space adjacent to the classified areas that allows access to the equipment to minimize maintenance and calibration personnel working in the classified areas. For example, autoclave, dry heat tunnels, or ovens could be installed in a manner that provides remote access to the equipment spaces. These gray spaces may comprise adjacent corridor access spaces or an interstitial space above the equipment and systems.

        

Maintenance sometimes involves opening areas that are not cleaned routinely (e.g., behind HEPA filters, electrical panels). If performed during operations, maintenance activities may increase the risk of product, environment, and equipment contamination. Routine maintenance reduces unexpected failures which, in turn, reduces the risk of contamination. Developing a control strategy for preventive and corrective maintenance is important to ensure that the validated state, product sterility, or contamination control is not compromised. The design of the equipment (single-use disposable versus multiuse) and the validated cleaning, disinfection, and sterilization processes, in conjunction with a comprehensive preventive maintenance plan, are critical components of the microbial control strategy.

        

If certain sections of the cleanroom need to be segregated for maintenance, temporary gray space enclosures (TGSE) can be considered instead of shutting down the entire cleanroom. TGSE requires careful planning and specific procedures to ensure controls are in place and being followed by maintenance personnel and contractors. Planning needs to define traffic patterns into and out of the TGSE area, include monitoring for pressure differential to ensure the enclosure is maintained at a pressure lower than the surrounding classified areas, and provide specific instructions to personnel for gowning and degowning as they enter and exit the TGSE area. The frequency and type of cleaning and sanitization activities performed around the TGSE could be increased to control contamination that may be associated with the TGSE and activities occurring there. Section 16.3 discusses a related case study.

        

Minimizing traffic in and around the TGSE area during operations is also important. Heightened EM around this area should be considered to provide information about whether the containment process is working as planned. Environmental data, such as airborne monitoring, that shows increased levels in the adjacent classified areas would indicate that the containment, personnel pathways, and gowning enhancements should be reassessed to improve the contamination control. Prior to setting up a maintenance TGSE, a process should be established to recover the area upon completion of those activities. This would typically include cleaning to remove any construction or gross contamination that may have occurred, followed by a comprehensive disinfection process to reestablish the environmental control. Depending on the specific maintenance or contamination activity, a specific cleaning and disinfection plan should be considered before releasing the areas for routine operation. For standard shut-down situations, it is common practice to perform a triple-cleaning and disinfection cycle followed by EM before releasing the areas for routine operation.

        

Devising a comprehensive preventive maintenance plan for parts that are reused, including elastomeric components (e.g., hoses, diaphragms, gaskets, O-rings), probes, agitators, valves, and filters, is crucial. Routine visual inspection of surfaces, including product contact surfaces, should be performed; such a program enables the early detection of rouging or any other deterioration of process equipment, which can prevent particulate contamination in the product and avoid the loss of cleaning effectiveness. The design of piping and valves should prevent steam condensate from collecting and possible backflow that might lead to contamination. Continuous assessments of change control, work orders, and other process improvements should be conducted to ensure that their individual or cumulative effects do not impact the CCS.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Maintenance (維護) 的雙面性：**TR90 揭示了維護活動的矛盾本質 — 定期維護可以預防設備故障和污染，但維護活動本身如果管控不當，也可能引入污染。這就是為什麼維護策略必須與 CCS 整合。

            

**Gray Space (灰色空間)：**建在潔淨區旁邊的非分級區域，讓維護人員可以從後方接觸設備，而不需要進入潔淨區。這是「設計消除風險」的最佳實踐。

            

**TGSE — Temporary Gray Space Enclosure (臨時灰色空間圍封)：**當潔淨室的部分區域需要進行維護時，可以建立臨時圍封而不是關閉整個潔淨室。這是在「維護需求」和「生產連續性」之間的平衡方案。

            

**Rouging (紅鏽)：**不鏽鋼設備表面因長期使用而產生的鐵氧化物沉積。會導致粒子污染並降低清潔效果。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

**TGSE = 餐廳裝修時的臨時隔板：**想像一家仍在營業的餐廳需要翻修廚房的一角。餐廳不會整間關門，而是用臨時隔板將施工區域與用餐區和其他廚房區域隔開。但這需要：

            

                
- 確保隔板密封良好（= 壓差監測）

                
- 施工人員有專用進出通道（= 定義交通動線）

                
- 施工人員穿戴防護裝備（= 更衣程序）

                
- 隔板周圍加強清潔（= 增加清潔消毒頻率）

                
- 施工完成後徹底清潔消毒才能恢復使用（= triple-cleaning cycle + EM）

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**TGSE 管控要點清單：**

            

                
- 定義人員進出動線

                
- 監測壓差（TGSE 區域壓力必須低於周圍分級區域）

                
- 專用更衣/脫衣程序

                
- 增加周圍清潔消毒頻率

                
- 加強 EM 監測

                
- 最小化 TGSE 周圍的人員流動

                
- 建立區域恢復程序

            

            

**Triple-Cleaning and Disinfection Cycle (三次清潔消毒循環)：**標準停機恢復做法。這不是一般的「清潔三次」，而是完整的「清潔 + 消毒」循環重複三次，之後還需要 EM 確認環境恢復合格才能放行。

        

        

            

#### 彈性體零件管理

            

TR90 特別強調 **Elastomeric Components (彈性體零件)**（墊圈、O-ring、隔膜、軟管等）的預防性維護計畫。這些零件是設備中最容易老化、劣化的部分，一旦失去密封功能就會成為污染入口。定期目視檢查產品接觸面可以早期偵測 rouging 或其他劣化，避免粒子污染和清潔效果下降。

        

        

            

#### 維護策略的風險平衡

            

```

維護策略考量：

  不做維護的風險：
    設備故障 → 非計畫停機 → 污染風險↑ → 產品損失

  維護本身的風險：
    開啟非常規區域 → 粒子/微生物釋放 → 環境污染

  最佳平衡點：
    預防性維護 (PM) > 矯正性維護 (CM)
    Gray space 設計 > 潔淨區內維護
    TGSE 區域隔離 > 整間潔淨室停機

  恢復標準：
    Triple clean/disinfect → EM 確認 → 放行
            
```

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 場景：**你的潔淨室 B 級區的一台 HVAC 風機需要緊急維修，但目前有兩條充填線正在進行商業批次生產。你決定使用 TGSE 方案。根據 TR90，你的行動計畫應包括：

            

                
1. 劃定 TGSE 範圍並安裝臨時圍封，確保壓差低於周圍 B 級區

                
2. 制定維護人員專用進出動線和更衣程序

                
3. 在 TGSE 周圍增加 EM 取樣點和取樣頻率

                
4. 增加 TGSE 周圍的清潔消毒頻率

                
5. 維修完成後執行 triple-cleaning cycle + EM 確認合格後才能放行該區域

                
6. 所有 EM 數據納入批次紀錄審查

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的工廠是否有 gray space 設計？如果沒有，哪些維護活動最常需要維護人員進入潔淨區？

                
2. 你的彈性體零件（O-ring、墊圈等）的更換頻率是如何決定的？是基於時間、使用次數還是狀態檢查？

                
3. 如果 TGSE 周圍的 EM 數據顯示微生物水準上升，你應該啟動哪些因應措施？

                
4. 請解釋為什麼 TR90 要求「持續評估變更管控、工單和其他製程改善的個別或累積效果」對 CCS 的影響。

            

        

    

    

### 本節重點回顧 Section Summary

    

        
- **整體性方法 (Holistic Approach)：**設備的「設計 → 確效 → 持續管控」必須作為一個完整的鏈條來規劃，三者環環相扣、缺一不可。「已確效」不等於「永遠有效」。

        
- **設計決定成本：**設備設計階段的投資可以大幅降低後續營運成本和風險。封閉系統、衛生級設計、互鎖機制、Gray space 等設計決策對 CCS 的長期成效影響深遠。

        
- **清潔確效的侷限性：**清潔確效的預測能力受限於測試時機、數量和方法。Biofilm（如 Arthrobacter russicus 可在 3 天內形成）是長期威脅。Clean hold time 管控是關鍵防線。

        
- **持續管控五大領域：**狀態管控、時間管控、完整性管控、正壓管控、轉運管控。每一項都有具體的查核要點。

        
- **SUS 與屏障技術：**SUS 提供封閉系統優勢但 integrity testing 受限；Barrier technology (Isolator/RABS) 是非封閉操作的首選；Product pathway 需進行 closure risk analysis。

        
- **維護的雙面性：**維護既是預防污染的手段，也是潛在的污染來源。TGSE 是平衡維護需求與生產連續性的有效工具，但需要嚴格的壓差、動線、EM 管控，以及 triple-cleaning cycle 恢復程序。

        
- **彈性體管理：**O-ring、墊圈等彈性體零件是設備密封的薄弱環節，需要納入預防性維護計畫。Rouging 等表面劣化的早期偵測可避免粒子污染。

    

    

PDA Technical Report No. 90: Contamination Control Strategy Development in Pharmaceutical Manufacturing

    

Section 9.0: Equipment Design, Validation, and Ongoing Control | Pages 30-34

    

Educational Material - For Training Purposes Only

↑

## Section 8: Containers & Closures 容器與密封 (p34-p37)

# Section 10.0 Product Containers and Closures

    

產品容器與密封系統

    

PDA Technical Report No. 90 | p34 - p37

    

### 本章學習目標

    

        
- 理解 Container Closure (CC) System（容器密封系統）在污染控制策略中的關鍵角色

        
- 掌握 Primary Container Closure（初級容器密封）的材質考量與微生物/微粒污染風險

        
- 了解 End-to-End Container Closure Integrity (CCI)（端到端容器密封完整性）的全面管控架構

        
- 認識 CCI 從設計開發、方法驗證到製程確認的完整生命週期管理

        
- 理解魚骨圖（Ishikawa Diagram）分析 CCI 影響因素的方法論

    

    

### 本節目錄

    

        10.0 Product Containers and Closures
        10.1 Primary Container Closures
        10.2 End-to-End CCI
        10.2.1 Design and Development
        10.2.2 CCIT Method Development
        10.2.3 CCI During Process Validation
    

10.0 Product Containers and Closures

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Container closure systems are an essential means of controlling microbial and foreign-particulate contamination of excipients, APIs, DS, process intermediates, and finished DPs (19). In the case of sterile products, a failure of container closure systems integrity may impact patient safety due to the potential for microbial ingress and product contamination. Throughout Section 10.0, the term container closure (CC) and packaging are used interchangeably.

        

            "A CC system is required to 'not be reactive, additive, or absorptive so as to alter the safety, identity, strength, quality, or purity of the drug beyond the official or established requirements.'"
        

        

In addition, the CC system should "provide adequate protection against foreseeable external factors in storage and use that can cause deterioration or contamination of the drug product" (20).

        

Therefore, the CC system should be designed to ensure that the material is protected from factors that may impact product quality over its shelf life, including light, evaporation, product loss, exposure to gases, absorption of water, or microbial and particulate contamination (21).

        

CC system for finished DP are frequently composed of primary and secondary container closures. The primary CC comes in direct contact with the DP and represents the main physical barrier preventing interaction of the product with the exterior environment. The CC system may include a delivery device assembled into the primary container closure for product functionality. Secondary packaging may help protect the primary CC system from microbial or foreign particulate contamination due to physical damage during handling and shipping.

        

CC system and the associated container closure integrity (CCI) is critical for the prevention of product contamination throughout the shelf life of a finished DP. Figure 10.2-1 provides an overview of CCI considerations.

        

Degrazio described in detail the main factors to consider when developing a CC system platform for sterile product packaging (22). Establishment of this framework is based on the six main aspects defined in a typical Ishikawa or fishbone diagram—materials, equipment, process, measurement, environment, and people (Figure 10.2-1).
